MMS 3 Energetic Particle Detector, Energetic Ion Spectrometer (EPD-EIS) Energy by Time of Flight, Level 2, Burst Survey

ResourceID
spase://VSPO/NumericalData/MMS/3/EnergeticParticleDetector/EIS/Burst/Level2/EnergyByTimeOfFlight/PT0.605S

Description

Energetic Particle Detector (EPD), Energetic Ion Spectrometer (EIS) Energy by Time of Flight, Level 2, Burst Survey, 0.605 s Data. The EIS provides ion composition measurements (protons versus oxygen ions) and angular distributions over the energy range from approximately 45 to 500 keV.

View XML | View JSON

ResourceID

ResourceHeader
ResourceName
MMS 3 Energetic Particle Detector, Energetic Ion Spectrometer (EPD-EIS) Energy by Time of Flight, Level 2, Burst Survey
ReleaseDate
2020-07-03 23:28:58Z
Description

Energetic Particle Detector (EPD), Energetic Ion Spectrometer (EIS) Energy by Time of Flight, Level 2, Burst Survey, 0.605 s Data. The EIS provides ion composition measurements (protons versus oxygen ions) and angular distributions over the energy range from approximately 45 to 500 keV.
